A copy of the Earnings Release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">The information in Item&#160;2.02 of this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> including Exhibit 99.1, is being furnished under Item&#160;2.02 and shall not be deemed to be &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Exchange Act</span></span>&#8221;), or otherwise subject to liability under that section, nor shall such information be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>onsemi Reports Record Second Quarter 2022 Results - Quarterly Revenue Exceeds $2B for the First Time </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>PHOENIX &#150; Aug. 1, 2022 &#150;</B> onsemi (the &#147;Company&#148;) (Nasdaq: ON) today announced results for the second quarter of 2022
with the following highlights: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Record revenue of $2,085.0&nbsp;million, an increase of 25&nbsp;percent year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Record GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross margin of 49.7&nbsp;percent
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GAAP operating margin of 28.0&nbsp;percent increased 1,110 basis points year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Record <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating margin of 34.5&nbsp;percent increased 1,490
basis points year-over-year </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GAAP diluted earnings per share of $1.02 as compared to $0.42 in the quarter a year ago </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share more than doubled year-over-year
to $1.34 from $0.63 on 25&nbsp;percent increase in revenue </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">LTM free cash flow margin of 17&nbsp;percent </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our ability to execute on our business transformation continues to deliver record revenue performance with 25&nbsp;percent year-over-year growth and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross margin expansion of 1,130 basis points to 49.7&nbsp;percent in the second quarter. These financial results validate our momentum in the market and the differentiation of our intelligent power and
sensing solutions. Our leadership in the accelerating megatrends of vehicle electrification, ADAS, energy infrastructure, and factory automation have enabled us to extend long term supply agreements and increase demand visibility. While we are
optimistic about our outlook, we remain sensitive to dynamic market conditions. The structural changes we implemented over the past eighteen months have reduced the volatility in our financials, and we have positioned the company to be more
resilient in all business environments.&#148; said Hassane <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">El-Khoury,</FONT> president and CEO of onsemi. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:20pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Selected

<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">*</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">Diluted shares outstanding can vary as a result of, among other things, the actual exercise of options or
vesting of restricted stock units, the incremental dilutive shares from the Company&#146;s convertible senior subordinated notes, and the repurchase or the issuance of stock or convertible notes or the sale of treasury shares. In periods when the
quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $20.72 for the 1.625% Notes and $52.97 for the 0% Notes, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share count and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income per
share include the anti-dilutive impact of the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 1.625% Notes and the 0% Notes, respectively. At an average stock price per share between $20.72 and $30.70 for the 1.625% Notes and $52.97
and $74.34 for the 0% Notes, the hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 1.625% Notes and 0% Notes, respectively. In periods when the quarterly average stock price exceeds $30.70 for the 1.625% Notes, and $74.34 for the 0%
Notes, the dilutive impact of the warrants issued concurrently with such notes are included in the diluted shares outstanding. GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share counts are based on either the previous
quarter&#146;s average stock price or the stock price as of the last day of the previous quarter, whichever is higher. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:24pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">**</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">Special items may include: amortization of acquisition-related intangibles; expensing of appraised inventory
fair market value <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">step-up;</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs, purchased <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-process</FONT> research and development expenses; restructuring,
asset impairments and other, net; goodwill impairment charges; gains and losses on debt prepayment; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> interest expense; actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits; and certain
other special items, as necessary. These special items are out of our control and could change significantly from period to period. As a result, we are not able to reasonably estimate and separately present the individual impact or probable
significance of these special items, and we are similarly unable to provide a reconciliation of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The reconciliation that is unavailable would include a forward-looking income statement,
balance sheet and statement of cash flows in accordance with GAAP.&nbsp;For this reason, we use a projected range of the aggregate amount of special items in order to calculate our projected <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating
expense outlook. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">***</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">We believe these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures provide important supplemental
information to investors. We use these measures, together with GAAP measures, for internal managerial purposes and as a means to evaluate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparisons.
However, we do not, and you should not, rely on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures alone as measures of our performance. We believe that <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures reflect an
additional way of viewing aspects of our operations that, when taken together with GAAP results and the reconciliations to corresponding GAAP financial measures that we also provide in our releases, provide a more complete understanding of factors
and trends affecting our business. Because <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are not standardized, it may not be possible to compare these financial measures with other companies&#146;
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, even if they have similar names. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>TELECONFERENCE </B></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About onsemi </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><B>onsemi</B> (Nasdaq: <FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" COLOR="#0000ff">ON</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">) is driving disruptive innovations to help build a better future. With a focus on automotive and industrial <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-markets,</FONT> the company is accelerating change in megatrends
such as vehicle electrification and safety, sustainable energy grids, industrial automation, and 5G and cloud infrastructure. <B>onsemi</B> offers a highly differentiated and innovative product portfolio, delivering intelligent power and sensing
technologies that solve the world&#146;s most complex challenges and leads the way to creating a safer, cleaner, and smarter world. <B>onsemi </B>is recognized as a Fortune 500<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> company and
included in the S&amp;P 500<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> index. Learn more about <B>onsemi</B> at </FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" COLOR="#0000ff">www.onsemi.com.</FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman"> </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"># # # </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">To supplement the consolidated financial results prepared in accordance with GAAP, onsemi uses
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">certain&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> which are adjusted from the most directly comparable GAAP measures to exclude items related to the amortization of intangible assets, amortization of acquisition-related
intangibles, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,&nbsp;inventory</FONT> valuation adjustments, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">purchased&nbsp;in-process&nbsp;research</FONT> and
development expenses, restructuring, asset impairments and other, net, goodwill impairment charges, gains and losses on debt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT> expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension
plans and other pension benefits, third party acquisition and divestiture-related costs, tax impact of these items and certain other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> items, as necessary. Management does not consider the effects
of these items in evaluating the core operational activities of onsemi. Management uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> internally to make strategic decisions, forecast future results and evaluate
onsemi&#146;s current performance. In addition, the Company believes that most analysts covering onsemi use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> to evaluate onsemi&#146;s performance. Given management&#146;s and
other relevant parties&#146; use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> onsemi believes these measures are important to investors in understanding onsemi&#146;s current and future operating results as seen
through the eyes of management. In addition, management believes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are useful to investors in enabling them to better assess changes in onsemi&#146;s core business across
different time periods. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">These&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are not prepared in accordance with, and should not be considered alternatives or necessarily superior to, GAAP financial data and may be different <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">from&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> used by other companies. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Because&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures are not standardized, it may not be possible to compare these financial
measures with other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">companies&#146;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures, even if they have similar names. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Revenue </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> revenue allows
management to evaluate, among other things, the revenue from the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent of special items. In addition,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-</FONT> GAAP revenue is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the
business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results. Management presents this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate
the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Gross</FONT> Profit and Gross Margin </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross</FONT> profit and gross margin allows management to evaluate, among other things, the gross margin and gross profit of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different
reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up</FONT> and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs. In addition, it is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and
reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate our revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of revenue of onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Operating</FONT> Income and&nbsp;Operating Margin </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;operating</FONT> income and operating margin allows management to evaluate,
among other things, the operating margin and operating income of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT>
including, generally speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs,&nbsp;amortization and impairments of
intangible assets, third party acquisition and divestiture-related costs, restructuring charges and certain other special items as necessary. In addition, it is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and
incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Net</FONT> Income Attributable to onsemi and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted
Earnings Per Share </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;net</FONT> income attributable to onsemi and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share allows management to evaluate the operating results of onsemi&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally, the amortization and impairments of intangible assets, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,</FONT> <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs, restructuring, gains and losses on debt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT> expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other
pension benefits, third party acquisition and divestiture-related costs, discrete tax items and other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> tax adjustments and certain other special items, as necessary. In addition, these items are
important components of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process, as they are used </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>NON-GAAP MEASURES (Continued) </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:8pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">
to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, setting targets and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures to enable investors and analysts to understand the results of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses and, to the extent comparable, to compare our results of
operations on a more consistent basis against those of other companies in our industry. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Free Cash Flow </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of free cash flow allows management to evaluate, among other things, the ability of the Company to make interest or principal payments
on its debt. Free cash flow is defined as the difference between cash flow from operating activities and capital expenditures disclosed under investing activities in the consolidated statement of cash flows. Free cash flow is not an alternate to
cash flow from operating activities as a measure of liquidity. It is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results
of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results. Management presents this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to enable investors and analysts to
evaluate our revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted Share Count </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted
share count allows management to evaluate, among other things, the potential dilution due to the outstanding stock options and restricted stock units excluding the dilution from the convertible notes that is covered by hedging activity up to a
certain threshold. In periods when the quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $20.72 for the 1.625% Notes and $52.97 for the 0% Notes, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share count includes the anti-dilutive
impact of the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 1.625% Notes and the 0% Notes, respectively. At an average stock price per share between $20.72 and $30.70 for the 1.625% Notes and $52.97 and $74.34 for the 0% Notes, the
hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 1.625% Notes and 0% Notes, respectively. In periods when the quarterly average stock price exceeds $30.70 for the 1.625% Notes, and $74.34 for the 0% Notes, the dilutive impact of the
warrants issued concurrently with such notes are included in the diluted shares outstanding. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>

</DIV></Center>
